/* <![CDATA[ */
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
      if (typeof ajaxurl === 'undefined') {
        ajaxurl = 'https://www.lodeate.it/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php'; // get ajaxurl
      }
      
        $('.shared-files-frontend-file-upload').submit(function (e) {

          let elem_class = $(this).closest('.shared-files-main-container').data('elem-class');

          if ($('.' + elem_class + ' .shared-files-file-metadata-entry').length == 0) {
            alert('Please choose the file first.');
            return false;
          }

        });
        

        var uploader = new plupload.Uploader({

          browse_button: 'browse-button',
          container: 'shared-files-file-uploader-container',

          url: 'https://www.lodeate.it/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',

          multipart_params: {
            'action': 'shared_files_file_upload',
            '_wpnonce': '8fcfd06b88',
          },

          multi_selection: ' . true . ',

          urlstream_upload: true,

          init: {

            FilesAdded: function(up, files) {

              plupload.each(files, function(file) {

                up.start();

                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').removeClass('shared-files-file-upload-status-error');
                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').removeClass('file-upload-status-ok');

                $('.shared-files-progress-bar-fill').addClass('shared-files-progress-bar-fill-active');

                $('.shared-files-progress-bar-fill').html('');

                $('.shared-files-progress-bar-fill').css('width', '');

                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').addClass('shared-files-file-upload-status-default');

              });

            },

            UploadProgress: function(up, file) {

              $('#' + file.id + ' b').html(file.percent + '%');

              $('.shared-files-progress-bar-fill').css('width', file.percent + '%');

              $('.shared-files-progress-bar-fill').html(file.percent + '%');


            },

            Error: function(up, err) {

              $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').html('<div>Error: ' + err.message + ' Status: ' + err.status + '</div>');

              console.log( err );

            },

            FileUploaded: function(up, file, response) {


              let res;

              try {
                res = JSON.parse(response.response);
              } catch (e) {
                console.error('Invalid server response', response.response);

                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').html('Upload failed: Invalid response from server.');

                return;
              }

              if (!res.success) {
                console.error('Server reported error:', res.data?.error || 'Unknown error');

                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').addClass('shared-files-file-upload-status-error');

                $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').html( 'Upload failed: ' + (res.data?.error || 'Unknown error') );

                return;
              }

              $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').addClass('file-upload-status-ok');

              var filename_parts = res.data.file.split('/');
              var filename = filename_parts.pop();

              $('.shared-files-file-upload-status').append( '<div>File uploaded: ' + filename + '</div>');

              var html = '<div class="shared-files-file-metadata-entry">' +
                  '<input type="hidden" name="_sf_file_uploaded_file[' + file.id + '][file]" value="' + res.data.file + '">' +
                  '<input type="hidden" name="_sf_file_uploaded_file[' + file.id + '][type]" value="' + res.data.type + '">' +
                  '<input type="hidden" name="_sf_file_uploaded_file[' + file.id + '][url]" value="' + res.data.url + '">' +
                  '<span>Uploaded (metadata): ' + file.name + '</span>' +
                  '</div>';

              $('#shared-files-file-metadata-entries').append(html);

              $('.shared-files-file-upload-status-next-steps').show();

            }

          }

        });

        uploader.init();

      });
//# sourceURL=shared-files-js-after

	<div class="mh-posts-grid-excerpt clearfix">
		<div class="mh-excerpt"><p>«Se l’uomo facesse abitualmente il segno della croce e invocasse più spesso la Madonna, diminuirebbero le sue tentazioni, perché il segno della croce è un mezzo per scacciare il diavolo e il nome della Madre <a class="mh-excerpt-more" href="https://www.lodeate.it/san-charbel-la-vita-le-opere-le-preghiere-documentario/" title="San Charbel &#8211; la vita, le opere, le preghiere &#8211; Documentario &#8211; Miracolo a Napoli">[Leggi tutto&#8230;]</a></p>
</div>	</div>
</article></div>
</div>

	<h3 class="entry-title mh-posts-grid-title">
		<a href="https://www.lodeate.it/misteri-e-prodigi-della-santa-casa-di-loreto-trasportata-degli-angeli/" title="Misteri e prodigi della Santa Casa di Loreto: TRASPORTATA DEGLI ANGELI!" rel="bookmark">
			Misteri e prodigi della Santa Casa di Loreto: TRASPORTATA DEGLI ANGELI!		</a>
	</h3>
	<div class="mh-meta entry-meta">
<span class="entry-meta-date updated"><i class="fa fa-clock-o"></i><a href="https://www.lodeate.it/2019/12/">10 Dicembre 2019</a></span>
<span class="entry-meta-comments"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><span class="mh-comment-count-link">Commenti disabilitati<span class="screen-reader-text"> su Misteri e prodigi della Santa Casa di Loreto: TRASPORTATA DEGLI ANGELI!</span></span></span>
</div>
	<div class="mh-posts-grid-excerpt clearfix">
		<div class="mh-excerpt"><p>Non è raro ascoltare, anche dalla labbra di chi dovrebbe essere guida nella fede, accenti scettici se non la negazione totale della possibilità stessa che Dio si possa essere servito di un miracolo per trasportare <a class="mh-excerpt-more" href="https://www.lodeate.it/misteri-e-prodigi-della-santa-casa-di-loreto-trasportata-degli-angeli/" title="Misteri e prodigi della Santa Casa di Loreto: TRASPORTATA DEGLI ANGELI!">[Leggi tutto&#8230;]</a></p>

</form><script type="text/javascript">
/* <![CDATA[ */

( ( dropdownId ) => {
	const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
	function onSelectChange() {
		setTimeout( () => {
			if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value && parseInt( dropdown.value ) > 0 && dropdown instanceof HTMLSelectElement ) {
				dropdown.parentElement.submit();
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "cat" );

//# sourceURL=WP_Widget_Categories%3A%3Awidget
/* ]]> */
</script>
